    </div>
    <div style="text-align: center; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">SANUWAVE Announces Q2 2023 Financial Results</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
    </div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">EDEN PRAIRIE, MN, AUGUST 11, 2023 &#8211; SANUWAVE Health, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221; or &#8220;SANUWAVE&#8221;) (OTCQB: SNWV), a leading provider of next-generation FDA-approved wound care
      products, today announced its 2nd quarter 2023 results.</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">For the three months ended June 30, 2023:</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" id="zb96158955bd2420296f5af186380bda7" class="DSPFListTable" style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; width: 100%; text-align: left; color: #000000;">

        <tr>
          <td style="width: 18pt; font-size: 10pt;"><br>
          </td>
          <td style="width: 18pt; vertical-align: top; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">&#9632;</td>
          <td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top; text-align: left; font-size: 10pt;">
            <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';">Revenue for the three months ended June 30, 2023 totaled $4.7 million, an increase of 20%, as compared to $3.9 million for the same period of 2022. This growth falls within the previously provided
              guidance range of 15-25% for Q2 2023. Revenue for the six months ended June 30, 2023 totaled $8.5 million, an increase of 19%, as compared to $7.1 million for the same period of 2022.</div>
          </td>
        </tr>

    </table>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" id="zbbdcbe9066be4225a45de19efae154d1" class="DSPFListTable" style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; width: 100%; text-align: left; color: #000000;">

        <tr>
          <td style="width: 18pt; font-size: 10pt;"><br>
          </td>
          <td style="width: 18pt; vertical-align: top; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">&#9632;</td>
          <td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top; text-align: left; font-size: 10pt;">
            <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';">49 UltraMist&#174; systems were sold in Q2 2023, up from 28 in Q1 of this year.</div>
          </td>
        </tr>

    </table>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" id="zf7f4cb4fe59f47cf8144720cde88f161" class="DSPFListTable" style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; width: 100%; text-align: left; color: #000000;">

        <tr>
          <td style="width: 18pt; font-size: 10pt;"><br>
          </td>
          <td style="width: 18pt; vertical-align: top; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">&#9632;</td>
          <td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top; text-align: left; font-size: 10pt;">
            <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';">UltraMist&#174; consumables revenue increased 25% to $2.8 million, versus $2.2 million for the same quarter last year on a 14% increase in treatments.&#160; Revenue growth outpaced treatments due to higher
              average sale prices.</div>
          </td>
        </tr>

    </table>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" id="z1e0ae7751166469ca44820a0f7412b8c" class="DSPFListTable" style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; width: 100%; text-align: left; color: #000000;">

        <tr>
          <td style="width: 18pt; font-size: 10pt;"><br>
          </td>
          <td style="width: 18pt; vertical-align: top; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">&#9632;</td>
          <td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top; text-align: left; font-size: 10pt;">
            <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';">UltraMist&#174; consumables revenue was 59% of overall revenue for Q2, up from 56% in the prior year period. This was primarily driven by a larger installed base, improved pricing, and higher usage rates.</div>
          </td>
        </tr>

    </table>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" id="z0037339f1ce84be2820c7549607a51f4" class="DSPFListTable" style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; width: 100%; text-align: left; color: #000000;">

        <tr>
          <td style="width: 18pt; font-size: 10pt;"><br>
          </td>
          <td style="width: 18pt; vertical-align: top; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">&#9632;</td>
          <td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top; text-align: left; font-size: 10pt;">
            <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';">Gross margin as a percentage of revenue increased to 74% for the three months ended June 30, 2023, vs 72% for the same period last year, primarily driven by stronger pricing initiatives.</div>
          </td>
        </tr>

    </table>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" id="z723a19172880430e9adf067c8070377f" class="DSPFListTable" style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; width: 100%; text-align: left; color: #000000;">

        <tr>
          <td style="width: 18pt; font-size: 10pt;"><br>
          </td>
          <td style="width: 18pt; vertical-align: top; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">&#9632;</td>
          <td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top; text-align: left; font-size: 10pt;">
            <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';">For the three months ended June 30, 2023, operating income totaled $0.9 million, which is an improvement of $4.0 million compared to the same period in 2022.&#160; This number benefited from a $1.25
              million one-time reversal of accrued expenses and was partially offset by a $224 thousand non-cash stock compensation issuance.</div>
          </td>
        </tr>

    </table>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" id="z82b10a957a394cdb9f74eb63db91c9fb" class="DSPFListTable" style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; width: 100%; text-align: left; color: #000000;">

        <tr>
          <td style="width: 18pt; font-size: 10pt;"><br>
          </td>
          <td style="width: 18pt; vertical-align: top; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">&#9632;</td>
          <td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top; text-align: left; font-size: 10pt;">
            <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';">Net loss for the three months ended June 30, 2023 was $7.3 million, compared to a net income of $1.6 million for the same period in 2022. The increase in net loss for the three months ended June 30,
              2023 was primarily due to continued non-cash losses on the fair value of derivative liabilities.</div>
          </td>
        </tr>

    </table>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" id="z643baff5c69543e6bcf0c9eb19ce3a8d" class="DSPFListTable" style="font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; width: 100%; text-align: left; color: #000000;">

          <td style="width: auto; vertical-align: top; text-align: left; font-size: 10pt;">
            <div style="font-family: 'Times New Roman';">The Company anticipates third quarter 2023 revenue growth will fall within a range of 15-25% as compared to the third quarter of 2022.</div>
          </td>
        </tr>

    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <div>
      <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">&#8220;We are pleased to have generated significant revenue growth in Q2 despite ongoing capacity constraints,&#8221; said CEO Morgan Frank. &#8220;It has been a challenging time at
        SANUWAVE, but as these results are beginning to show, our drive toward cost cutting, process optimization, and margin expansion is beginning to gain traction as we move toward our near-term goals of growth acceleration and operating profitability.&#160;
        In the coming quarters, we aim to continue and build upon this trend as we break the production and supply chain logjams that have prevented us from realizing the potential of the UltraMist system.&#8221;</div>
      <div style="font-size: 10pt;"><br>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div>
      <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(41, 56, 73); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">Guidance</div>
      <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
      <div style="text-align: left; color: rgb(41, 56, 73); font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">The Company continued to have constrained inventory supply during Q2 2023 and anticipates this will improve in Q3, but remain a significant
        factor. The Company anticipates Q3 2023 revenue growth of approximately 15% to 25% year over year. SANUWAVE its constrained inventory supply will improve materially and enable an acceleration of revenue growth in Q4 2023.</div>

    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt; font-weight: bold;">About SANUWAVE</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">SANUWAVE Health is focused on the research, development, and commercialization of its patented, non-invasive and biological response-activating medical systems for the
      repair and regeneration of skin, musculoskeletal tissue, and vascular structures.</div>
    <div style="font-size: 10pt;">&#160;</div>
    <div style="text-align: left; font-family: 'Times New Roman'; font-size: 10pt;">SANUWAVE&#8217;s end-to-end wound care portfolio of regenerative medicine products and product candidates help restore the body&#8217;s normal healing processes. SANUWAVE applies and
      researches its patented energy transfer technologies in wound healing, orthopedic/spine, aesthetic/cosmetic, and cardiac/endovascular conditions.</div>
